
            INSERT INTO dara_mallas_study_plan_line
                (line_order,
                area_homologation_id,
                study_plan_id,
                company_id
            )
            SELECT
                '10' AS line_order,
                ah.id AS area_homologation_id,
                sp.id AS study_plan_id,
                4 AS company_id
            FROM dara_mallas_study_plan sp

            JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                ON p.id = sp.program_id
            AND p.company_id = 4

            JOIN dara_mallas_program_code pc
                ON pc.program_id = p.id
            AND pc.company_id = 4
            AND pc.name = 'UAME1P020'

            JOIN dara_mallas_area_homologation ah
                ON ah.area_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_area
                    WHERE code = '020-C01'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.company_id = 4

            WHERE sp.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
            )
            AND sp.company_id = 4

            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM dara_mallas_study_plan_line spl
                WHERE spl.study_plan_id = sp.id
                AND spl.area_homologation_id = ah.id
                AND spl.company_id = 4
            );

        
            INSERT INTO dara_mallas_study_plan_line

                ah.id AS area_homologation_id,
                sp.id AS study_plan_id,
                4 AS company_id
            FROM dara_mallas_study_plan sp

            JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                ON p.id = sp.program_id
            AND p.company_id = 4

            JOIN dara_mallas_program_code pc
                ON pc.program_id = p.id
            AND pc.company_id = 4
            AND pc.name = 'UAME1P014'

            JOIN dara_mallas_area_homologation ah
                ON ah.area_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_area
                    WHERE code = '014-C06'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.company_id = 4

            WHERE sp.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
            )
            AND sp.company_id = 4

            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM dara_mallas_study_plan_line spl
                WHERE spl.study_plan_id = sp.id
                AND spl.area_homologation_id = ah.id
                AND spl.company_id = 4
            );

                ON p.id = sp.program_id
            AND p.company_id = 4

            AND pc.company_id = 4
            AND pc.name = 'UAME1P001'

            );

        
            INSERT INTO dara_mallas_study_plan_line
                (line_order,
                area_homologation_id,
                study_plan_id,
                company_id
            )
            SELECT
                '90' AS line_order,
                ah.id AS area_homologation_id,
                sp.id AS study_plan_id,
                4 AS company_id
            FROM dara_mallas_study_plan sp

            JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                ON p.id = sp.program_id
            AND p.company_id = 4

            JOIN dara_mallas_program_code pc
                ON pc.program_id = p.id
            AND pc.company_id = 4
            AND pc.name = 'UAME3L554'

            JOIN dara_mallas_area_homologation ah
                ON ah.area_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_area
                    WHERE code = 'L554-M9'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.company_id = 4

            WHERE sp.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
            )
            AND sp.company_id = 4

            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM dara_mallas_study_plan_line spl
                WHERE spl.study_plan_id = sp.id
                AND spl.area_homologation_id = ah.id
                AND spl.company_id = 4
            );

        
            INSERT INTO dara_mallas_study_plan_line
                (line_order,
                area_homologation_id,
                study_plan_id,
                company_id
            )
            SELECT
                '100' AS line_order,
                ah.id AS area_homologation_id,
                sp.id AS study_plan_id,
                4 AS company_id
            FROM dara_mallas_study_plan sp

            JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                ON p.id = sp.program_id
            AND p.company_id = 4

            JOIN dara_mallas_program_code pc
                ON pc.program_id = p.id
            AND pc.company_id = 4
            AND pc.name = 'UAME3L554'

            JOIN dara_mallas_area_homologation ah
                ON ah.area_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_area
                    WHERE code = 'L554-M10'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
                )
            AND ah.company_id = 4

            WHERE sp.period_id = (
                    SELECT id
                    FROM dara_mallas_period
                    WHERE name = '000000'
                    AND company_id = 4
            )
            AND sp.company_id = 4

            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1
                FROM dara_mallas_study_plan_line spl
                WHERE spl.study_plan_id = sp.id
                AND spl.area_homologation_id = ah.id
                AND spl.company_id = 4
            );
